occurred just after the disaster central sulawesi itself according output data belonging the ministry women empowerment and child protection ranks fifth amerika serikat the city with the cases child marriage wahana visi indonesia wvi which has assisted area central sulawesi carrying out various activities suppress this number this done because child marriages have serious consequences for children such amerika serikat stunting wvi has taken two approaches suppress numbers even completely eradicate child marriages namely through the application parenting with love parents and doing policy advocacy wvi also has partnerships with many groups jointly solusi child marital problems one them with the palu city indonesian ulema council create parenting with love module islamic context considering the mayoritas central sulawesi residents are muslims not only majelis ulama indonesia but wvi also has similar cooperation with other child groups and organizations and involves religious and traditional leaders prevention efforts must complemented regulations regional regulations together with other organizations will encourage the birth the child marriage prevention law said ronny ichwan the advocacy team the response the wvi disaster central sulawesi related this initiation sukarti head the protection women and special protection for children central sulawesi province gave positive signal through the regional regulation draft regional regulation draft carried out the coalition the central sulawesi legislative council also supports the creation the regional regulation partnership company smart class for children papua company smart class for children papua feb the learning activity inside samsung smart learning class samsung smart learning class sslc established biak papua yayasan pendidikan kristen ypk waupnor elementary school october sslc was result collaboration wahana visi indonesia and samsung elektronik indonesia support education for children east indonesia after the inauguration sslc has been using the students biak district for now the local government the education ministry and gki papua education foundation have managed the activity sslc there are several parts that are carried out before this class operates order support the program that presents technology for the learning process the classroom socialization and support for strengthening community roles have been carried out through the selection school committee administrators the school committee was chosen because bridge the role parents support sslc and school education programs training has also been given about the main roles and tasks the school committee maximize the running the program sslc wahana visi indonesia together with several partners also participated training for teachers improve the skills teachers when using technology sslc teachers and students participated the training facilitated pesona edu jakarta through this training teacher competence increasingly equipped ensure quality teaching process that the target increasing student literacy skills achieved present sslc accessed students every day from the schedule that has been made other schools whose teachers have attended training are given the opportunity access this class every saturday maria kendi teacher ypk waupnor elementary school said that she really liked this class including the children she taught the full range facilities provided this class helps maria engage interesting learning process according him internet support and technology make teaching and learning activities more attractive written jhon eris purba area program manager biak wahana visi indonesia related articles sep decreasing stunting breastfeeding the number stunting palu central the village level the movement encourage open and participatory government realize innovative solutions for communities open government action plan from bloro village one wahana visi indonesia wvi assisted villages talking about open government this week bloro village chosen amerika serikat one its models said johny noya wvi area program manager sikka district the opening the citizen meeting friday march according him the village has implemented three pillars the open government namely transparency participation and innovation the activity the continuation the meeting held every thursday night two sub-villages bloro village this special day the villagers were invited participate measuring the performance the village government pemdes through filling out the scoring cards warga desa bloro mengisi kartu penilaian terkait pengurusan akta kelahiran anak the session this citizen meeting was the launch the village administration revenue and expenditure budget apbdes followed the question and answer session between villagers and the village head people receive information about budgets need financed during this fiscal year soter sani nurak explained the information brochures were shared with all citizens world health organization attended the meeting unfortunately until now have not received the money yet added also mentioned that the budget was based the results deliberations the hamlet level level also with posyandu cadres and the village child forum after that the launching public services the village through the suggestion box and call center text message amerika serikat proof transparency citizen participation and innovation the bloro village government chairman the village consultative body bpd wendelinus emuardus said that this effort was change and improvement hopefully the citizens will use suggestion box and call center properly voice their aspirations yance padeng the head nita sub-district showed his highest appreciation bloro village government his opinion the three things that have been achieved this village effort fulfill children basic are triggering the ownership the birth certificate having access clean water and the involvement children the process community discussion about local development needs musrenbang also thank wvi for facilitating citizen meeting and the activities child forum this collaboration has gabungan goro sambut tds kabupaten solok nov wib pemerintahan keterangan gambar apel gabungan goro sambut tds arosuka kominfo wakil gubernur sumbar nasrul abit didampingi bupati solok diwakili asisten ekbangkesra medison memimpin jalannya apel gabungan gotong royong dermaga danau singkarak jumat hadir kepala skpd lingkungan propinsi sumatera barat asisten staf ahli bupati kepala skpd camat lingkungan pemerintah kabupaten solok forkompimda kabupaten solok wali nagari salingka danau singkarak medison sambutannya ucapan selamat wakil gubernur kawasan dermaga danau singkarak salah destinasi wisata kabupaten solok medison kegiatan apel dilanjutkan kegiatan gotong royong kawasan danau singkarak kegiatan kegiatan rutin dilaksanakan menjaga kebersihan lingkungan menyambut event tour adik singkarak diakhir sambutannya medison menginformasikan peserta apel pemerintah propinsi sumatera barat membentuk badan pengelola kawasan danau singkarak berbasis nagari goro dipimpin wakil gubernur sumbar mari bersepakat menjaga danau singkarak menjaga kebersihan danau menyelamatkan nelayan mata pencahariannya danau singkarak himbau nasrul abit diawal sambutannya nasrul abit masyarakat salingka danau singkarak nelayan menumbuhkan malu membuang sampah kah danau menjaga ekosistem menertibkan bagan ikan admin social media share this article tags pemerintahan write facebook comment tuliskan muaro paneh periode resmi dilantik kabupaten solok sep wib adat agama keterangan gambar ketua muaro paneh periode resmi dilantik arosuka kominfo wakil gubernur sumatera barat nasrul abit didampingi wakil bupati solok yulfadri nurdin resmi melantik ketua muaro paneh periode sdn muaro paneh sabtu hadir ketua dewan perwakilan rakyat daerah kabupaten solok jon firman pandu kabiro hubungan masyarakat propinsi sumatera barat jasman camat bukit sundi forkompimcam bukit sundi wali nagari se-kecamatan bukit sundi tokoh masyarakat bundo kanduang se-kabupaten solok yuli hariadi malin panduko laporannya tujuan kegiatan mengukuhkan pati ambalau muaro paneh bundo kanduang periode kepengurusan dilantik orang diakhir laporannya yuli ucapan terimakasih donatur berpartisipasi mensukseskan kegiatan elson rajo gamuyang ketua dilantik diawal sambutannya harapannya kepengurursan membimbing kemenakan memahami aturan adat segi berpakaian bertingkah laku memahami norma-norma adat berlaku nagari mari bangun nagari menguatkan peran mamak keluarga mengarahkan kemenakan kah arah positif elson diakhir sambutannya ucapkan selamat angku-angku niniak mamak pemangku adat nagari muaro paneh dikukuhkan pengurus kerapatan adat nagari kedepan semoga amanah diemban dilaksanakan yulfadri mengawali sambutannya yulfadri pengurus berperan aktif penyelenggaraan pemerintah ditingkat nagari tingkat kabupaten bidang pelestarian adat yulfadri niniak mamak pemangku adat kepengurusan pemimpin didahuluan salangkah ditinggian sarantiang yulfadri menghimbau pengurus dilantik menjalin komunikasi tokoh adat tokoh agama tokoh masyarakat diakhir sambutannya yulfadri pemerintah daerah sangat mendukung rencana program pengurus bersifat positif mempu membangun kabupaten solok perjelas identitas masyarakat minangkabau kental adat berpedoman agama bertekad melestarikan adat budaya minangkabau sumatera barat narul abit diawal sambutannya nasrul mengajak mengenalkan generasi muda adat budaya adat minangkabau nasrul depannya bangso dilaksanakan program peningkatan kesejahteraan masyarakat nagari sumani bangso musyawarah kali dibahas permasalahan nagari mencari solusi penyelesaiannya muhammad leon sambutannya
